name:C‚Äço‚Äçn‚Äçg‚Äçl‚Äçi‚Äçn‚Äça‚Äçf‚Äçu
info:Deluxe Double Room
info:Stayed in October 2023
info:Business travelers
info:3 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted October 24, 2023
msg:I stayed in the deluxe king room of Hilton Hotel Zhengzhou for three days. When I checked out, I had an inexplicable urge to stay another day. This is the most cost-effective hotel I have stayed in in the past few years, bar none.

It was my first time to go to Zhengzhou and I was not familiar with it. I took a taxi from Zhengzhou East Railway Station. In fact, after getting off the high-speed rail, you can take the subway directly to Yanzhuang Station. The hotel is not far from the subway station, which is very convenient. The hotel is on Jinshui Road. There is Manhattan Plaza across from the overpass. The street is full of small restaurants, offering various tastes. But if you want to eat well, it feels more reliable to stay in a hotel.

After checking in, a fruit plate was delivered to the room, which felt very good. The fruit combination is not only beautiful but also delicious. It is obviously carefully selected and washed very clean, which is great.

The mattress in the double bed room is extremely thick, and the bed is very tall as a whole. It's a little awkward for a person who is not very tall to sit on the edge of the bed with his feet unable to reach the ground. The softness and firmness of this mattress are perfect, and the quilt and pillows are very dry, making it so comfortable to sleep on. For three nights, I turned on the reading light and fell asleep without paying attention, and slept until dawn. For middle-aged people like me who don't sleep well, when buying a mattress, you can really refer to the mattress specifications of this hotel.

Thumbs up for the desk and computer chair in the room. I did a lot of work on the computer in the room. The leader and myself are very satisfied with the results of this business trip.

The sound insulation effect of the room is generally good. The carpet is very thick and the walls seem to be soft-covered. Anyway, I didn't hear the sound from upstairs and next door at all. However, the soundproofing of the door is average, and you can hear people talking loudly in the corridor.

The toilet and bathroom are quite satisfactory, with plenty of hot water. The sink area is large. There is a large bathtub next to it, which is very comfortable to take a bath. The drain cover in the bathtub doesn't work very well, maybe I don't understand how to use it. There are all the small appliances such as a kettle and hair dryer, and the tea bags and instant coffee are of good quality.

I changed rooms once and stayed on both the 12th and 26th floors. The rooms are equally nice inside. The view from the upper floors is better, but there are many high-rise buildings around. Unless you live on a particularly high floor, there is no need to spend extra money to stay on the middle floor, because you can't see too far away.

I have not experienced the various public facilities in the hotel this time, so I will not comment on them. It is said that there is a swimming pool. There seems to be a business bar on the 37th floor. I guess it would be nice to drink some wine in the evening and take a look at the night view in the distance.

There is a large restaurant on the first floor of the hotel. There is a breakfast buffet in the morning and a dinner buffet in the evening. It is highly recommended to add a breakfast coupon when staying here. Regardless of Chinese or Western breakfast, the variety, quality and taste are amazing. I really like the spicy soup here and drank two bowls of it every day for three consecutive days. Fried dough sticks, pancakes and fruit, big meat buns, fried eggs, the delicious Chinese breakfast is dazzling. Western-style breakfast focuses on cold food, there are many varieties, and they all look delicious. The baguette here must be cut into two slices, and the pine nut brown bread is spread with butter. The texture and taste are very authentic, and the quality of the bread is not inferior to that of foreign bakeries. After a full breakfast, I have a cup of Americano coffee without sugar, which is so comforting.

If you have a big appetite, we recommend the evening buffet. There are a lot of hard dishes, including steaks, lamb chops, seafood, and this season there are also full-yellow hairy crabs, so feel free to eat! ! Not to mention the ingredients and cooking skills, the Chinese, French and Japanese cuisines are all on point. It‚Äôs really great value for money. I might have happened upon them doing an event, and I was given a gift of Buddha Jumping over the Wall, French foie gras and lobster, which was a luxury. There are many kinds of drinks, and I have a good impression of the red wine there, but unfortunately I forgot to see what brand it was. The red wine is very smooth in the mouth, with just the right sweetness and acidity, and goes well with seafood and steak. The buffet is so rich that it‚Äôs easy to lose control of your appetite. If you eat too much, your stomach will become bloated and a bit uncomfortable, so you must control yourself. In addition, it is sad to see many people take too much and end up with a lot of food on the plate and throw it away.
